!module config:qinq.
!QinQ: Qinq profile config-----------------------------------
!
!QinQ: Olt qinq domain config-----------------------------------
!---------------------------------------------------------------
!Basic command format:
!create oltqinq_domain <name>
!set oltqinq_domain <name> service_num <number>
!set oltqinq_domain <name> <1-8> uprule {<1-27> <value> <op>}*4 {serv_id <1-8>}*1
!set oltqinq_domain <name> <1-8> downrule {<1-27> <value> <op>}*4
!set oltqinq_domain <name> <1-8> {vlan <1-4> [<oldvid>|null] [<oldcos>|null] [add|translation|transparent] <tpid> [<cos>|null] [<newvid>|null]}*4
!Key parameter interpretation:
!<1-8>: service index.
!<1-27>: 1: Destination MAC. 2: Source MAC. 3: Ethernet Type. 4: Fourth layer VLAN. 5: Third layer VLAN. 6: Second layer VLAN. 7: First layer VLAN. 8: TOS. 10: TTL. 11: Protocol type. 12: Source IPv4. 13: Source IPv6. 14: Destination IPv4. 15: Destination IPv6. 16: L4 source port. 17: L4 destination port. 18: Cos4. 19: Cos3. 20: Cos2. 21: Cos1. 22: Destination IPv6 prefix. 23: Source IPv6 prefix. 24: IP version. 25: IPv6 traffic class. 26: IPv6 flow label. 27: IPv6 next header.
!<op>: 0: Never. 1: ==. 2: !=. 3: <=. 4: >=. 5: Exist. 6: No exist. 7: Always.
!---------------------------------------------------------------
!
!QinQ: Onu attach olt qinq config-----------------------------------
!
!QinQ: Pon attach olt qinq config-----------------------------------
!
!QinQ: Onu qinq policing config-----------------------------------
!
!QinQ: Gpon vlan table config-----------------------------------

!
!QinQ: Qinq parameters config-----------------------------------
!
!QinQ: Pon attach vlan table config-----------------------------------
